debug_decisions = {
	TUR_trigger_check = {
		allowed = { always = yes }
		available = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_legitimacy = 0
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_reload_minority_values = {
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = ALB
				tag = ARA
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes }
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_reload_centralization_values = {
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = ALB
				tag = ARA
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { ottoman_centralization_variable_check = yes }
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_update_party_popularities = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
			TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_right = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				value = 2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = 2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_left = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				value = -2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = -2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
}

GER_great_war = {
	TUR_offer_surrender_terms = {
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		activation = {
			check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 25 }
			has_capitulated = no
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
			is_subject = no
			any_country = {
				is_major = yes
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					surrender_progress > 0.4
					# war is losing
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							has_capitulated = yes
						}
						faction_leader = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
					}
				}
				# so fucked
				AND = {
					has_war_support < 0.2
					has_stability < 0.2
				}
				# Constantinople lost
				NOT = { controls_state = 347 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess }
					has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_government_stability_at_least_25
				check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var > 24 }
			}
			controls_state = 347
			surrender_progress < 0.4
			has_war_support > 0.2
			has_stability > 0.2
			NOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess }
					has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_war = no
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = { TUR_armistice_of_mudros_effect = yes }
	}
	TUR_retreat_from_occupied_areas_caucasus = {
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		activation = { always = no }
		selectable_mission = yes
		cancel_trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser } }
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { has_state_flag = TUR_treaty_of_batum_state } }
		complete_effect = {
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = TUR
				set_country_flag = kars_republic
				hidden_effect = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = kars_republic
					set_stability = 0.85
					set_war_support = 0.78
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = { remove_core_of = KRS }
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_treaty_of_batum_state }
						add_core_of = KRS
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								tag = TUR
								is_subject_of = TUR
							}
						}
						has_state_flag = TUR_treaty_of_batum_state
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_create_kars_republic
					hidden_effect = { transfer_state_to = KRS }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_possible_country = {
						limit = { has_character = KRS_ibrahim_aydin }
						KRS_ibrahim_aydin = {
							set_nationality = KRS
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = { ideology = revolutionary_socialism }
							}
						}
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = yes
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					set_popularities = {
						neutrality = 38
						fascism = 28
						communism = 10
						democratic = 24
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = KRS_party
						long_name = KRS_party
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						name = KRS_party
						long_name = KRS_party
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism
						name = KRS_party
						long_name = KRS_party
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						name = KRS_party
						long_name = KRS_party
					}
					load_focus_tree = empty_focus
					set_research_slots = 2
					set_capital = {
						state = 806
						remember_old_capital = no
					}
				}
				give_military_access = PREV
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							any_owned_state = { any_neighbor_state = { has_state_flag = TUR_treaty_of_batum_state } }
							has_country_flag = defeated_TUR_in_great_war
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = defeated_TUR_in_great_war
					is_major = yes
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = topple_government
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = TUR_retreat_from_occupied_areas_caucasus_2_month_timer
			}
		}
	}

	TUR_declare_jihad = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		available = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_major = yes
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
			OR = {
				has_idea_with_trait = tgwr_caliph
				has_country_leader_with_trait = tgwr_caliph
			}
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_idea_with_trait = tgwr_caliph
				has_country_leader_with_trait = tgwr_caliph
			}
		}
		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			add_war_support = 0.05
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_muslim_state = yes
					has_resistance = yes
				}
				add_compliance = 3
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_controlled_state = {
								is_muslim_state = yes
								has_resistance = yes
							}
						}
						every_controlled_state = {
							limit = {
								is_muslim_state = yes
								has_resistance = yes
							}
							add_compliance = 15
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_muslim = yes }
						add_war_support = 0.1
					}
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_controlled_state = {
								is_muslim_state = yes
								has_resistance = yes
							}
						}
						every_controlled_state = {
							limit = {
								is_muslim_state = yes
								has_resistance = yes
							}
							add_resistance = 15
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_muslim = yes }
						add_war_support = -0.1
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_jihad_declared
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_declare_jihad_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_morale_factor = 0.02 }
			set_variable = { TUR_aoabe_weekly_casualties_war_support = 0.002 }
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = ottoman.232 hours = 6 } }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1000
		}
	}

	TUR_lift_the_armenian_reforms = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_break_treaty
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		cost = 50
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise }
					ARA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise
					any_owned_state = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_yenikoy_accord
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_vilayet
							has_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_vilayet_no_control
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RUS } }
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
							has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
							has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
						}
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_van
							has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
							has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
							has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
						}
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
								has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
								has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
								has_state_flag = TUR_van
								has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
								has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
								has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
							}
						}
						clr_state_flag = TUR_yenikoy_accord
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR } }
							clr_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_vilayet_no_control
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				end_puppet = ARA
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ARA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser } } }
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ottoman.217 hours = 8 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = probably_lead_to_war_with_rus_tt
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_lift_the_armenian_reforms
			ottoman_armenian_variable_check_only = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = great_war
				any_enemy_country = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_revolting_country } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS = { has_war = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_establish_order_in_macedonia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_police_action
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		cost = 10
		state_target = yes
		targets = {
			345
			731
			184
			788
			225
			759
			1141
			203
			1213
			106
			1140
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 45
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_law_on_churches
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority }
				}
				NOT = { has_state_flag = TUR_established_order_in_macedonia }
			}
		}
		available = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				type = infantry
				size > 2
				state = FROM
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { controls_state = FROM }
				divisions_in_state = {
					type = infantry
					size < 3
					state = FROM
				}
			}
        }
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { state = 345 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_establish_order_in_macedonia_tt1
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek = -0.05 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 731
							state = 184
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_establish_order_in_macedonia_tt2
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek = -0.1 }
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_south_slavic = -0.1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 788
							state = 225
							state = 759
							state = 1141
							state = 203
							state = 1213
							state = 106
							state = 1140
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_establish_order_in_macedonia_tt3
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_south_slavic = -0.2 }
				}
				add_compliance = -10
				set_state_flag = TUR_established_order_in_macedonia
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

					value = -0.05

			}
		}

				every_state = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_commander_in_chief_visit scope = TUR } }

		}

			base = 15
		}
	}

		}

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TUR_government_committee_struggle } }

					id = TUR_government_committee_struggle

							id = TUR_mufrit_struggle
							value < 0
						}

						value = 0.05

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_break_treaty

		visible = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA }
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_focus_tree = ottoman_focus_tree }
				always = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_focus_tree = ottoman_syria_focus_tree }
				has_completed_focus = TRS_dissolve_the_debt_council
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_OPDA_trigger_tooltip
				has_variable = opda_consumer_goods
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = debt_less_than_0
				check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < 0 }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPDA_idea }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPDA_idea
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPDA_idea_2 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPDA_idea_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea_2 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea_3 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_3
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA }
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_dissolved_OPDA
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
	}

	TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul = {
		icon = oil
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = export_focus
				has_idea = free_trade
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
			676 = {
				controller = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_full_control_of_state = PREV
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_kirkuk
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_baghdad
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_basra
			}
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 676 } }
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = TUR_turkish_petroleum_company_decision_time?120
		visible = { has_completed_focus = TUR_found_the_turkish_petroleum_company }
		complete_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { TUR_add_debt_1_ENG = yes }
				50 = { TUR_add_debt_1_GER = yes }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			676 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 2 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 5 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 9 compare = less_than }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 2 compare = equals } }
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul
					bonus = 0.3
					uses = 1
					category = synth_resources
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 5 compare = equals } }
				676 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 9 compare = equals } }
				676 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals } } }
				set_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 0 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 1 }
		}
	}

				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}

	TUR_investments_from_BEL = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = BEL
				var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
				BEL = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
					}
					else = { NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission } }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = { BEL = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans } }
		activation = { always = no }
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = yes
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { BEL = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_inBELstructure } }
				var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = inBELstructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_3_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BEL = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
				var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_5_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BEL = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { BEL = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military } }
					var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { BEL = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:BEL.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_7_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { BEL = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					BEL = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}

					limit = { USA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_milUSAry } }
					var:USA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { USA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:USA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_7_USA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { USA = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					USA = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_investments_from_RUS = {
		icon = GFX_decision_RUS_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = RUS
				var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
				RUS = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
					}
					else = { NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission } }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = { RUS = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans } }
		activation = { always = no }
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = yes
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_inRUSstructure } }
				var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = inRUSstructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_3_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
				var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_5_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_milRUSry
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_milRUSry } }
					var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:RUS.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_7_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					RUS = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	invest_in_ottoman_rumelia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }

				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_rumelia
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		fire_only_once = no
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				TUR_investment_state_rumelia = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TUR = { any_owned_state = { TUR_investment_state_rumelia = yes } }
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_at_all
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_rumelia
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = ottoman.40

			set_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 5
				factor = 0
			}

				num_of_civilian_factories > 10
				add = 2
			}

				num_of_civilian_factories > 15

			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 20
				add = 2

				num_of_civilian_factories > 25

				num_of_civilian_factories > 30

				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 25
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 50
				}
				add = 3

				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 80

				add = 3

				add = -10

		}

	invest_in_ottoman_syria = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = TUR } }
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_syria
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_tt
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		fire_only_once = no
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				TUR_investment_state_syria = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TUR = { any_owned_state = { TUR_investment_state_syria = yes } }
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_at_all
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_syria
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = ottoman.42
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
			set_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 5
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 10
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 15
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 20
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 25
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 30
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 25
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 50
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 80
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_together_with = TUR
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = RUS
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}

TUR_intelligence_market = {
	TUR_steal_classified_documents = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SWI_expand_covert_operations
		allowed = { NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" } }
		visible = { has_completed_focus = TUR_officialize_the_second_bureau }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { is_major = yes } }
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_tech = advanced_cryptanalysis } }
				has_tech = decryption_machine
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_tech = basic_cryptanalysis } }
				has_tech = advanced_cryptography
			}
			else = { has_tech = basic_cryptanalysis }
		}
		days_remove = 70
		cost = 50
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_steal_classified_documents_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = TUR_stolen_documents }
					FROM = { add_to_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents = 1 } }
					add_to_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents_ROOT = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					FROM = { set_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents = 1 } }
					set_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents_ROOT = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 20 }
	}
	TUR_sell_off_intelligence_reports = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SWI_expand_covert_operations
		allowed = { always = yes }
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_officialize_the_second_bureau
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}
		target_trigger = { FROM = { is_major = yes } }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_sell_off_intelligence_reports_tt
				check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents_ROOT > 1 }
			}
		}
		cost = 35
		days_re_enable = 90
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_to_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents_ROOT = -1 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_sell_off_intelligence_reports_tt2
			FROM = { country_event = { id = ottoman.249 hours = 8 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
			event_option_tooltip = ottoman.250.a
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 35 }
	}
	TUR_purchasing_intelligence_reports = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_exchange_intelligence_data
		allowed = { always = yes }
		days_remove = 90
		visible = { has_decision = TUR_purchasing_intelligence_reports }
		complete_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -1 }
			var:TUR_selling_intelligence_tag = { add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			var:TUR_selling_intelligence_tag = { add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -1 } }
		}
	}
	TUR_utilize_intelligence_reports = {
		allowed = { always = yes }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents > 1 } } }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_utilize_intelligence_reports_tt
				FROM = { check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents > 1 } }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { FROM =  { add_to_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents = -1 } } }
			add_decryption = {
				target = FROM
				amount = 50
			}
			add_intel = {
				target = FROM
				civilian_intel = 5
				army_intel = 5
				navy_intel = 5
				airforce_intel = 5
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_government = democratic
						FROM = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						FROM = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = fascism
						FROM = { NOT = { has_government = fascism } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = communism
						FROM = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				FROM = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				FROM = { has_added_tension_amount > 10 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				FROM = { has_added_tension_amount > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_railway
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				original_tag = ARM
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				controls_state = 939
			}
		}
		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				}
				is_subject = no
				has_capitulated = no
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					owns_state = 939
					controls_state = 939
					owns_state = 823
					controls_state = 823
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 5
		remove_effect = { FROM = { give_military_access = ROOT } }
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
	}
